17,913 feet (5,460 meters), and on October 2, 2009 released the drilling rig for
use on the Elijah #3 well and temporarily suspended operations on the
Ma'anit-Rehoboth #2 well, until a smaller rig becomes available for completion
operations on the seven zones that warrant completion testing.</font></div>

I noted that four of the zones are in the upper (Triassic) part of the hole and

drilled in the Ma'anit-Rehoboth #2 well.</font></div>

testing procedures.</font></div>

rights offering, stockholders have the right to purchase twenty three (23)
shares of stock for every one hundred (100) shares of common stock owned on the
record date.&#160;&#160;This is identical to 0.23 subscription rights for each
share of common stock owned on the record date.</font></div>

$5.00 shares as you subscribed for in the earlier rights offering, this is your
